<P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Shareholder Meeting Notice </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Amazon.com, Inc.&#146;s Annual Meeting of Shareholders will be held on May 23, 2013 at the Seattle Repertory Theatre, 155 Mercer Street, Seattle, Washington 98109, at 9:00 a.m. Pacific
Time. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Proposals to be voted on at the meeting are listed below along with the Board of Directors&#146;
recommendations. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">The Board of Directors recommends a vote FOR all nominees listed in Proposal 1 and FOR
Proposal 2. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">1. ELECTION OF DIRECTORS </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Nominees: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">1a. Jeffrey P. Bezos </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">1b. Tom A. Alberg </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">1c. John Seely Brown </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">1d. William B. Gordon
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">1e. Jamie S. Gorelick </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">1f. Alain Moni&eacute; </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">1g. Jonathan J. Rubinstein
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">1h. Thomas O. Ryder </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">1i. Patricia Q. Stonesifer </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">2. RATIFICATION OF THE
APPOINTMENT OF ERNST &amp; YOUNG LLP AS INDEPENDENT AUDITORS </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">The Board of Directors recommends a vote AGAINST
the following proposal: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">3. SHAREHOLDER PROPOSAL REGARDING A REPORT CONCERNING CORPORATE POLITICAL
CONTRIBUTIONS </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">PLEASE NOTE - YOU CANNOT VOTE BY RETURNING THIS NOTICE. To vote your shares you must vote online
or by telephone or request a paper copy of the proxy materials to receive a proxy card. If you wish to attend and vote at the meeting, please bring this notice with you, or other proof of ownership as of the record date, and government issued photo
identification. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Amazon.com, Inc. 2013 Annual Meeting </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Directions to the Amazon.com, Inc. 2013 annual meeting are available at www.amazon.com/ir </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Here&#146;s how to order a copy of the proxy materials and select a future delivery preference: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Paper copies: Current and future paper delivery requests can be submitted via the telephone, Internet or email options
below. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Email copies: Current and future email delivery requests must be submitted via the Internet following
the instructions below. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">If you request an email copy of current materials you will receive an email with a
link to the materials. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">PLEASE NOTE: You must use the number in the shaded bar on the reverse side when
requesting a set of proxy materials. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Internet - Go to www.envisionreports.com/amzn. Click Cast Your Vote or
Request Materials. Follow the instructions to log in and order a copy of the current meeting materials and submit your preference for email or paper delivery of future meeting materials. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Telephone - Call us free of charge at 1-866-641-4276 and follow the instructions to log in and order a paper copy of the
materials by mail for the current meeting. You can also submit a preference to receive a paper copy for future meetings. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Email - Send email to investorvote@computershare.com with &#147;Proxy Materials Amazon.com, Inc.&#148; in the subject line. Include in the message your full name and address, plus the
number located in the shaded bar on the reverse, and state in the email that you want a paper copy of current meeting materials. You can also state your preference to receive a paper copy for future meetings. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="line-height:0pt;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman" SIZE="1" COLOR="#FFFFFF">To facilitate timely delivery, all requests for a paper copy of the proxy materials must be received by May 13, 2013.
